## THE BINDING RULE (this is the contract the diff must satisfy)

A source may be DELETED from the grounding pool ONLY when:
- it is a CHROME non-source (failed fetch: bot/captcha/cookie/404/login/empty), OR
- the topic judge produced a FRESH `OFF_SUBJECT` verdict THIS run.

And ALL of these must hold:
1. A weight/reranker label (`content_relevance_label = demoted` / `escalated_demoted`) can NEVER trigger a delete. It is a weight-demote-to-0.25 KEEP label (a Qwen3-Reranker numeric score / a GLM "INSUFFICIENT" entailment), not a topic verdict.
2. A positive relevance verdict (`content_relevance_label in {relevant, escalated_relevant}`) VETOES deletion unconditionally — even against a stale/false OFF stamp. When the two judges disagree, positive relevance wins.
3. FRESH-VERDICT-ONLY: a stale `OFF_SUBJECT` stamp reloaded from an earlier run's `corpus_snapshot` (judge did NOT re-run this pass) must demote-KEEP, never delete.
4. `OFF_ASPECT` (same subject entity, wrong aspect — a topic-adjacent hub) is demote-KEEP, NEVER deletable. Only `OFF_SUBJECT` (clearly different subject) is deletable. A legacy bare `OFF` maps to `OFF_ASPECT` (conservative).
5. FAIL-OPEN on ANY uncertainty / missing verdict / stale-only stamp / error / non-Mapping row => KEEP. A predicate bug must never delete a source.
6. No credible ON-TOPIC source is deletable — not by tier, lexical guess, or a breadth number.
7. Disclosure is DURABLE + per-source + lands on the Methods section + the manifest summary; a deletion is never silent (§-1.3.1 fail-loud).
Chrome is a SEPARATE leg from off-topic (both a stamp-side clear and a topic-side skip) so a garbled/bot body can never be mislabeled `confirmed_offtopic`.
Faithfulness engine (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role D8 / provenance) must be BYTE-UNTOUCHED. Every fix must be a default-ON flag that is byte-identical when OFF. No caps/targets/thinners (the §-1.3 day-waster ban).

## Per-file summary vs the Fable fix plan (Fixes 1-6)

`src/polaris_graph/generator/junk_deletion_gate.py` — Fix 1 + Fix 2 + Fix 5 (records):
- NEW `is_row_deletable_offtopic(row, fresh_off_subject_ids=None)`: the default-ON delete predicate. Deletes ONLY on `_stamped_off_subject(row)` (topic judge OFF_SUBJECT). Positive `content_relevance_label` returns False (unconditional veto) BEFORE any OFF check. `content_relevance_label` is NEVER read as a delete trigger. Fresh-set gate (Fix 2): a concrete `fresh_off_subject_ids` set + `PG_DELETE_OFFTOPIC_FRESH_VERDICT_ONLY` ON => a row whose `evidence_id` is not in the set demote-KEEPs. `None` => freshness un-enforced (byte-identical Fix-1). Wrapped in try/except => fail-open KEEP.
- `_stamped_off_subject`: True only on `topic_off_subject is True` / string tokens / `topic_relevance_verdict == "off_subject"`. Legacy `topic_offtopic_demoted` alone does NOT count.
- `partition_rows` gains `fresh_off_subject_ids`; chrome-first if/elif preserved; default-ON branch calls `is_row_deletable_offtopic` and emits reason `confirmed_offtopic_subject`; legacy `is_row_confirmed_offtopic` reachable ONLY behind `PG_DELETE_OFFTOPIC_TOPIC_JUDGE_ONLY=0`.
- `disclosure_records`: adds `tier`, `signal`, `judge_verdict` per source.
Two new kill-switches (`topic_judge_only_deletion_enabled`, `fresh_verdict_only_deletion_enabled`), both default ON.

`src/polaris_graph/retrieval/topic_relevance_gate.py` — Fix 3 + Fix 4 (topic-side):
- Fix 3: `PG_TOPIC_GATE_SUBJECT_ASPECT_SPLIT` (default ON). `_build_batch_prompt(..., subject_aspect_split=)` returns a 3-verdict contract (`ON | OFF_ASPECT | OFF_SUBJECT`) when ON; the else-branch reproduces the legacy 2-verdict prompt byte-for-byte. NEW `_parse_batch_verdicts_split` (bare `off` -> OFF_ASPECT conservative; separator-tolerant; fail-open None on count mismatch). In `classify_topic_relevance`: OFF_SUBJECT rows get `topic_off_subject=True`; OFF_ASPECT + ON rows `pop("topic_off_subject", None)` to CLEAR a STALE True baked into corpus_snapshot (Codex-P1 gate-fix — prevents a stale True re-entering the fresh set).
- Fix 4 (topic-side): `PG_JUNK_CHROME_BEFORE_OFFTOPIC` (default ON). `_row_is_chrome_nonsource` uses the pure content-integrity detector on the widest body; a chrome row is skipped from the judge entirely (never stamped off_subject), kept in `sources` for the chrome-delete leg. `chrome_skipped=N` added to notes.

`scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py` — Fix 2 seam + Fix 4 (stamp-side) + Fix 5 + Fix 6 token:
- Fix 2 seam: `_fresh_off_subject_ids` bound to `set()` BEFORE the gate block (always bound on every path to the seam); filled from `_topic_result.demoted_rows where topic_off_subject is True`; threaded into `partition_rows(..., fresh_off_subject_ids=_fresh_off_subject_ids)`.
- Fix 4 stamp-side: on a confirmed chrome row set `topic_off_subject = False` (belt-and-suspenders to partition_rows' chrome-first) so chrome_nonsource stays honest.
- Fix 5: NEW `_attach_junk_deletion_disclosure(manifest, run_dir)` reads the durable `junk_deletion_disclosure.json`, splits `deleted_chrome_nonsources` (reason startswith `content_integrity_junk`) vs `deleted_offtopic_sources` (reason startswith `confirmed_offtopic` — catches BOTH `confirmed_offtopic_subject` AND legacy `confirmed_offtopic`; the OLD success-only filter used `== "confirmed_offtopic"` and silently MISSED the Fix-1 reason). Called inside `_attach_tool_utilization` (single pre-write chokepoint) so it lands on EVERY manifest write. The timeout finalizer now also routes through `_attach_tool_utilization`. Durable `junk_deletion_disclosure.json` written at the seam on every exit path. Report `## Methods — source hygiene` line appended to the reliability APPENDIX (not the scored body).
- Fix 6 token: topic judge `max_tokens` now `PG_SCOPE_TOPIC_MAX_TOKENS` (default 1200 byte-identical; manifest sets 16000) to un-starve a reasoning scope model (§9.1.8).

`.codex/I-deepfix-001/LAUNCH_READINESS_BOTH_BOXES.md` — Fix 6 launcher hygiene (BOTH box1 + box2 halves): removed `PG_OFFTOPIC_RELEVANCE_OVERRIDE=0`; added `PG_DELETE_OFFTOPIC_TOPIC_JUDGE_ONLY=1 PG_DELETE_OFFTOPIC_FRESH_VERDICT_ONLY=1 PG_TOPIC_GATE_SUBJECT_ASPECT_SPLIT=1 PG_JUNK_CHROME_BEFORE_OFFTOPIC=1` explicit; kept `PG_RESUME_RUN_TOPIC_JUDGE=1` (a plain resume must re-stamp fresh OFF_SUBJECT verdicts or Fix 2 suppresses ALL off-topic deletion); added `PG_SCOPE_TOPIC_MAX_TOKENS=16000`.

Tests: `tests/polaris_graph/test_junk_deletion_gate.py` (+143), `test_od_seam_complete.py` (new +217), `test_topic_gate_subject_aspect_split_od.py` (new +278).

## Embedded core diffs

### junk_deletion_gate.py
```diff
@@ is_row_deletable_offtopic (new default-ON predicate) @@
def is_row_deletable_offtopic(row, fresh_off_subject_ids=None):
    try:
        if not isinstance(row, Mapping):
            return False
        label = str(row.get("content_relevance_label", "") or "").strip().lower()
        if label in _POSITIVE_RELEVANCE_LABELS:   # {relevant, escalated_relevant}
            return False  # positive relevance — KEEP (unconditional veto)
        if not _stamped_off_subject(row):
            return False
        if fresh_off_subject_ids is not None and fresh_verdict_only_deletion_enabled():
            eid = str(row.get("evidence_id", "") or "")
            if eid not in {str(e) for e in fresh_off_subject_ids}:
                return False  # stale stamp — demote-keep
        return True
    except Exception:
        return False  # fail-open KEEP

@@ partition_rows off-topic branch @@
elif offtopic_on:
    if topic_judge_only_deletion_enabled():        # default ON
        if is_row_deletable_offtopic(row, fresh_off_subject_ids=fresh_ids):
            reason = "confirmed_offtopic_subject"
    elif is_row_confirmed_offtopic(row):           # legacy, only when flag OFF
        reason = "confirmed_offtopic"
```

```diff
        n_chrome_skipped += 1; continue               # never judged, never off_subject

elif v == "OFF_ASPECT": offtopic_rows.append(row); offaspect_rows.append(row)
elif v == "ON": ontopic_rows.append(row)
# after batches (split ON):

if split:
    for row in offaspect_rows: row.pop("topic_off_subject", None)  # clear STALE True
    for row in ontopic_rows:   row.pop("topic_off_subject", None)
```

## THE GENUINE (NON-EFFORT) RISKS — the ONLY things that could stop us beating both
These are real and must be de-risked EARLY (measure-first), because build effort cannot make them go away:

MITIGATION: every synthesized sentence span-checked against EVERY cited basket + NLI-entailment + contradiction-edge gate; if it can't be verified it ships as a labeled author-summary or not at all. THIS is the #1 bet.

3. **Self-inferred-rubric coverage (the planner bet):** the DuMate-style planner infers its OWN coverage rubric (never the gold) — does it actually cover the gold categories? If it systematically misses, coverage caps. MITIGATION: diverse/multi-perspective rubric generation; measure recall vs gold on the sample.

  152: def _row_is_chrome_nonsource(row: dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
  153:     """True iff the CONTENT-INTEGRITY detector confirms this row is a chrome non-source
  154:     (bot/captcha/cookie/404/login/empty). Reads a pre-existing ``content_integrity_junk``
  155:     stamp first (cheap), else runs the pure leaf detector on the WIDEST body + url + title
  156:     (the long-body Zyte-recovery guard inside the detector protects a real source whose title
  157:     is a stale bot page). FAIL-OPEN: any import / error / non-dict => False (row is judged
  158:     normally — a detector bug must never silently skip a real source)."""
  159:     try:
  160:         if not isinstance(row, dict):
  161:             return False
  162:         v = row.get("content_integrity_junk")
  163:         if bool(v) and str(v).strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "no", "off", ""):
  164:             return True
  165:         from src.tools.access_bypass import (  # noqa: PLC0415
  166:             detect_content_integrity_junk as _detect_ci_junk,
  167:         )
  168:         body = max(
  169:             (str(row.get(_bk) or "") for _bk in _CHROME_BODY_FIELDS),
  170:             key=len, default="",
  171:         )
  172:         url = str(row.get("source_url") or row.get("url") or "")
  173:         title = str(row.get("title") or row.get("source_title") or row.get("statement") or "")

  175:         return bool(is_junk)
  176:     except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — a detector defect must never skip a real source
  177:         return False

  213: 
  214: 
  215: def _row_title_text(row: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  216:     """Title-like text accessor mirroring evidence_selector._row_title_text.
  217: 
  218:     Live evidence rows populate ``statement`` with ``cand.title[:300]`` (not
  219:     ``title``). Precedence: explicit ``title`` > ``statement`` >
  220:     ``source_title`` > "". Returns a plain string (never None)."""
  221:     for key in ("title", "statement", "source_title"):
  222:         v = row.get(key)
  223:         if isinstance(v, str) and v:
  224:             return v
  225:     return ""
  226: 
  227: 
  228: def _row_snippet_text(row: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
  229:     """Short snippet for the topic judgement. Uses ``snippet`` /
  230:     ``direct_quote`` (whichever is present), bounded to _MAX_SNIPPET_CHARS."""
  540:     exempt_rows: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
  541:     judged_rows: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
  542:     judged_meta: list[tuple[str, str]] = []  # (title, snippet) per judged row
  543:     # I-deepfix-003 (#1374) Fix 4 (topic-side): chrome non-sources are NOT judged (nothing real
  544:     # to judge) — tracked separately so they never inflate the marquee-``exempt`` telemetry, and
  545:     # they stay in ``sources`` so the DEFAULT keep-all path still returns them (the chrome-delete
  546:     # leg removes them later). Read the flag ONCE.
  547:     chrome_skip = junk_chrome_before_offtopic_enabled()
  548:     n_chrome_skipped = 0
  549:     for row in sources:
  550:         if _is_exempt(row):
  551:             exempt_rows.append(row)
  552:             continue
  553:         if chrome_skip and _row_is_chrome_nonsource(row):
  554:             # A failed fetch, not a source — never judge it, never stamp it off-topic.
  555:             n_chrome_skipped += 1
  556:             continue
  557:         title = _row_title_text(row)
  558:         snippet = _row_snippet_text(row)
  559:         if not title and not snippet:

  561:             exempt_rows.append(row)

  564:         judged_meta.append((title, snippet))
  565: 
  566:     # Confident-OFF verdicts are accumulated in the loop. The kept set is
  567:     # computed once below preserving the caller's ORIGINAL order — critical
  568:     # because `evidence_for_gen` arrives already ranked best-first (relevance x
  569:     # authority) and there is NO re-rank between this gate and the generator.
  570:     # Partitioning exempt/kept to the end would push high-value marquee / anchor
  571:     # rows to the tail of the list the generator sees (a real regression on the
  572:     # gate-ON acceptance path).
  573:     #
  574:     # I-deepfix-001 (§-1.3 WEIGHT, DON'T FILTER — the operator names the "scope
  575:     # hard-filter" as a BANNED anti-pattern; the ONLY hard gate is the
  576:     # faithfulness engine): a confident-OFF source is, BY DEFAULT, KEPT in the
  577:     # pool and DEMOTED (disclosed off-topic via the ``topic_offtopic_demoted``
  578:     # sidecar), NEVER hard-dropped. Topicality is a WEIGHT — the source still
  579:     # flows to composition where the UNCHANGED strict_verify / NLI / 4-role
  580:     # engine is the only gate. The legacy hard-drop is preserved behind
  581:     # ``PG_SCOPE_TOPIC_GATE_HARD_DROP`` (audit / reversal). Order is unchanged in
  582:     # BOTH modes (no tail-partition), so a demoted row stays best-first-ranked.
  583:     hard_drop = topic_gate_hard_drop_enabled()
  584:     rescue_on_stamp = os.environ.get("PG_TOPIC_GATE_RESCUE_ON_STAMP", "1").strip().lower() not in (
  585:         "0", "false", "no", "off",
  586:     )
  587:     # I-deepfix-003 #1374 Fix 3: split the OFF verdict into OFF_ASPECT (demote-keep) vs
  588:     # OFF_SUBJECT (the only deletable OFF). Default ON; OFF = byte-identical legacy prompt
  589:     # + two-verdict parser + no ``topic_off_subject`` sidecar.
  590:     split = topic_gate_subject_aspect_split_enabled()
  591:     offtopic_rows: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
  592:     offtopic_titles: list[str] = []
  593:     ontopic_rows: list[dict[str, Any]] = []  # I-deepfix-001: confident-ON, for the rescue False-stamp
  594:     # I-deepfix-003 Fix 3: confident-OFF_SUBJECT rows (a subset of offtopic_rows) — the
  595:     # ONLY rows that receive the deletable ``topic_off_subject=True`` sidecar. Empty
  596:     # unless the subject/aspect split is enabled.
  597:     offsubject_rows: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
  598:     # I-deepfix-003 gate-fix (Codex P1): confident-OFF_ASPECT rows (same entity, wrong
  599:     # aspect — demote-KEEP, NEVER deletable). Tracked so the deletable ``topic_off_subject``
  600:     # sidecar can be CLEARED to False on them (demote path below) — a STALE True baked into
  601:     # corpus_snapshot by an earlier run must NEVER survive on a row THIS run re-verdicts
  602:     # OFF_ASPECT (it would be misread as a fresh OFF_SUBJECT and deleted). Empty unless the
  603:     # subject/aspect split is enabled.
  604:     offaspect_rows: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
  605: 
  606:     for start in range(0, len(judged_rows), size):
  607:         end = min(start + size, len(judged_rows))
  608:         batch_rows = judged_rows[start:end]
  609:         batch_meta = judged_meta[start:end]
  610:         batch = [

  612:             for local_idx in range(len(batch_rows))

  616:             research_question, batch, subject_aspect_split=split,

  618:         try:

  620:         except Exception as exc:  # FAIL-OPEN on any LLM error -> keep batch.

  624:             )

  628:         else:
  629:             verdicts = _parse_batch_verdicts(raw, expected)
  630:         if verdicts is None:  # FAIL-OPEN on count mismatch / unparseable.
  631:             _LOGGER.warning(
  632:                 "[scope] topic_gate batch unparseable / count mismatch — "
  633:                 "fail-open, keeping %d sources", len(batch_rows),
  634:             )
  635:             continue
  636:         for local_idx, row in enumerate(batch_rows):
  637:             v = verdicts.get(local_idx)
  638:             if split:

  640:                 # OFF_SUBJECT additionally carries the deletable sidecar below.
  641:                 if v == "OFF_SUBJECT":

  643:                     offtopic_titles.append(batch_meta[local_idx][0] or "(no title)")

  647:                     offtopic_titles.append(batch_meta[local_idx][0] or "(no title)")

  659:                 # but never CLEAR a stale bad stamp baked into the corpus_snapshot by an earlier run.
  660:                 # Stamping False on a confident-ON verdict lets a fixed-prompt re-judge un-bury the

  664:                 ontopic_rows.append(row)
  665: 
  666:     if hard_drop:
  667:         # LEGACY (explicit opt-in): hard-drop the confident-OFF set.
  668:         _off_ids = {id(r) for r in offtopic_rows}
  669:         kept_rows = [r for r in sources if id(r) not in _off_ids]

  671:         demoted_rows: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
  672:         demoted_titles: list[str] = []
  673:     else:
  674:         # DEFAULT (§-1.3 keep-all + demote): KEEP every source (original order),
  675:         # disclose the confident-OFF set as DEMOTED, and stamp a faithfulness-
  676:         # neutral sidecar so a downstream weighter can sink it WITHOUT dropping.
  677:         kept_rows = list(sources)
  678:         for row in offtopic_rows:

  680:         # I-deepfix-001 (drb_72): RESCUE — stamp False on confident-ON rows so a fixed-prompt
  681:         # re-judge CLEARS a stale bad True baked into the corpus_snapshot by an earlier run.
  682:         # Gated PG_TOPIC_GATE_RESCUE_ON_STAMP (default ON); OFF => no False stamp = byte-identical.
  683:         if rescue_on_stamp:

  685:                 row["topic_offtopic_demoted"] = False

  689:         # deletable). The downstream junk-deletion gate keys deletion on this sidecar.
  690:         for row in offsubject_rows:
  691:             row["topic_off_subject"] = True

  707:             for row in ontopic_rows:
  708:                 row.pop("topic_off_subject", None)

  715:         f"{verb}={len(offtopic_rows)} exempt={len(exempt_rows)} "

    1: """GH I-deepfix-003 (#1374) — junk-deletion grounding gate.
    2: 
    3: Operator rule change 2026-07-09 (CLAUDE.md §-1.3.1): the §-1.3 never-DROP rule is
    4: LIFTED for genuine JUNK. Weighting junk to zero is insufficient — a zero-weight row
    5: still sits in the evidence pool, the bibliography, and the per-claim corroboration
    6: counts, where it pollutes a clinical report (a bot-detection page anchoring a claim; a
    7: predatory PDF padding the count; an off-topic law/tourism source). Two classes are
    8: hard-DELETED from the run-level grounding pool BEFORE generation:
    9: 
   10:   (a) CHROME NON-SOURCES — bot/captcha/cookie/404/login/empty pages. A failed fetch is
   11:       not a source. The content-integrity detector stamps ``row["content_integrity_junk"]``
   12:       upstream (the re-tier seam); this gate deletes the stamped rows.
   13:   (b) SEMANTICALLY-CONFIRMED OFF-TOPIC whole sources — a source a SEMANTIC topic judge
   14:       confirmed off-topic to the research question. DEFAULT path (Fix 1,
   15:       ``is_row_deletable_offtopic``) deletes ONLY on the topic judge's affirmative
   16:       OFF_SUBJECT stamp: a weight/reranker ``content_relevance_label``
   17:       (``demoted`` / ``escalated_demoted``) can NEVER delete, and a positive relevance
   18:       verdict (``relevant`` / ``escalated_relevant``) vetoes deletion UNCONDITIONALLY. Judge
   19:       verdict ONLY, FAIL-OPEN (any uncertainty / missing verdict / error => KEEP), never a
   20:       lexical/tier/number rule. The legacy weight-label reuse
   21:       (``weighted_enrichment._is_confirmed_offtopic`` via ``is_row_confirmed_offtopic``) is
   22:       reachable only behind ``PG_DELETE_OFFTOPIC_TOPIC_JUDGE_ONLY=0`` (byte-identical OFF).
   23: 
   24: STILL BINDING (§-1.3): credible ON-TOPIC sources, even low-tier / social / non-journal,
   25: are NEVER deleted here (they are neither content-junk nor confirmed-off-topic). An
   26: off-topic SPAN inside an on-topic source is handled at compose (the span screen), not
   27: here. Duplicates consolidate elsewhere. The faithfulness engine is UNTOUCHED — deleting a
   28: row can only SHRINK the grounding pool, so a claim citing a deleted junk row FAILS
   29: strict_verify (it can never make one PASS). A deleted junk row was never a valid anchor.
   30: 
   31: MARQUEE/CONTRACT EXEMPTION: a required-entity / contract-bound anchor is on-topic by
   32: construction and is NEVER deleted (its evidence_id is in ``exempt_ids``), mirroring the
   33: topic gate's existing anchor exemption.
   34: 
   35: Deletion is DISCLOSED: every deleted row is RETURNED with its reason for the manifest + a

  141:     subject (the DELETABLE class of the OFF split, e.g. a scholar-mill / tourism / religion
  142:     page in an AI-labor report). The Fix-3 sidecar is the bool ``topic_off_subject=True``; a

  155: 
  156: def is_row_deletable_offtopic(
  157:     row: Mapping[str, Any],
  158:     fresh_off_subject_ids: "Iterable[str] | None" = None,
  159: ) -> bool:
  160:     """DELETE predicate for the confirmed-off-topic class (topic-judge-only path, Fix 1 + Fix 2).
  161: 
  162:     Returns True (row is DELETABLE) iff the topic judge AFFIRMATIVELY stamped this WHOLE
  163:     source OFF_SUBJECT. Three hard guarantees keep this from over-deleting:
  164: 
  165:     * A weight/reranker ``content_relevance_label`` (``demoted`` / ``escalated_demoted``) is
  166:       NEVER a delete trigger — those are weight-demote-to-0.25 KEEP labels (a Qwen3-Reranker
  167:       numeric score / a GLM 'INSUFFICIENT' entailment), NOT topic verdicts. Reusing them as a
  168:       DELETE trigger is exactly what hard-deleted 197 on-topic rows (St. Louis Fed, OECD, ILO,
  169:       McKinsey, HBS, Wikipedia, 23 T1 journal papers) in the I-deepfix-003 pass.
  170:     * An affirmative positive-relevance verdict (``content_relevance_label`` in
  171:       {relevant, escalated_relevant}) VETOES deletion UNCONDITIONALLY — even against a
  172:       stale/false OFF stamp. When the two judges disagree, the positive relevance wins.
  173:     * Fix 2 (fresh-verdict-only): when ``fresh_off_subject_ids`` is supplied (a concrete set —
  174:       the evidence_ids THIS run's topic judge freshly confirmed OFF_SUBJECT) AND
  175:       ``PG_DELETE_OFFTOPIC_FRESH_VERDICT_ONLY`` is ON, a row whose OFF_SUBJECT stamp is NOT in
  176:       that set is a STALE snapshot stamp (an earlier run's verdict reloaded from
  177:       corpus_snapshot) and demote-KEEPs — only a fresh verdict deletes. ``None`` (the default)
  178:       => freshness is un-enforced (byte-identical to the Fix-1-only path).
  179: 
  180:     FAIL-OPEN: not a Mapping / no OFF_SUBJECT stamp / stale-only stamp / missing verdict / any
  181:     error => NOT deletable (row KEPT). A predicate bug must NEVER delete a source."""
  182:     try:
  183:         if not isinstance(row, Mapping):
  184:             return False
  185:         label = str(row.get("content_relevance_label", "") or "").strip().lower()
  186:         if label in _POSITIVE_RELEVANCE_LABELS:
  187:             return False  # affirmative positive-relevance verdict — KEEP (unconditional veto)
  188:         if not _stamped_off_subject(row):
  189:             return False
  190:         # Fix 2: a STALE snapshot OFF_SUBJECT stamp (not in this run's fresh set) demote-KEEPs.
  191:         # Enforced only when the caller passes a concrete set AND the flag is ON.
  192:         if fresh_off_subject_ids is not None and fresh_verdict_only_deletion_enabled():
  193:             eid = str(row.get("evidence_id", "") or "")
  194:             if eid not in {str(e) for e in fresh_off_subject_ids}:
  195:                 return False  # stale stamp — demote-keep, never delete on an old verdict
  196:         return True
  197:     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — never delete on a predicate bug
  198:         logger.warning(
  199:             "[junk_deletion_gate] deletable-offtopic predicate errored (%s) — row KEPT "
  200:             "(fail-open).", str(exc)[:160],
  201:         )
  202:         return False
  203: 
  204: 
  205: def partition_rows(
  206:     rows: list[dict[str, Any]],
  207:     exempt_ids: "Iterable[str] | None" = None,
  208:     fresh_off_subject_ids: "Iterable[str] | None" = None,
  209: ) -> tuple[list[dict[str, Any]], list[dict[str, Any]]]:
  210:     """Split the run-level grounding pool (``evidence_for_gen``) into
  211:     ``(kept, deleted)``.
  212: 
  213:     A row is DELETED iff it is a chrome non-source (kill-switch A) OR a
  214:     confirmed-off-topic source (kill-switch B), AND its ``evidence_id`` is NOT in
  215:     ``exempt_ids`` (a marquee / contract-bound anchor is on-topic by construction and is
  216:     never deleted). Each deleted row carries a ``deletion_reason`` for disclosure.
  217: 
  218:     Order-preserving; never mutates the input rows (a deleted row is copied before the
  219:     reason is stamped); idempotent (re-running on a clean pool returns it unchanged with
  220:     an empty deleted list). When BOTH kill-switches are OFF, returns ``(list(rows), [])``
  221:     — byte-identical.
  222:     """
  223:     chrome_on = chrome_deletion_enabled()
  224:     offtopic_on = offtopic_deletion_enabled()
  225:     if not chrome_on and not offtopic_on:
  226:         return list(rows), []
  227:     exempt = {str(e) for e in (exempt_ids or ())}
  228:     # Fix 2: materialize the fresh OFF_SUBJECT id set ONCE (or None to leave freshness
  229:     # un-enforced). A stale-stamp row whose id is absent demote-KEEPs (see
  230:     # is_row_deletable_offtopic).
  231:     fresh_ids = None if fresh_off_subject_ids is None else {str(e) for e in fresh_off_subject_ids}
  232:     kept: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
  233:     deleted: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
  234:     for row in rows:
  235:         if not isinstance(row, Mapping):
  236:             kept.append(row)
  237:             continue
  238:         eid = str(row.get("evidence_id", "") or "")
  239:         if eid and eid in exempt:
  240:             kept.append(row)  # marquee / contract anchor — NEVER deleted
  241:             continue
  242:         reason = ""
  243:         if chrome_on and is_row_content_junk(row):
  244:             reason = "content_integrity_junk:" + str(
  245:                 row.get("content_integrity_class", "chrome") or "chrome"
  246:             )
  247:         elif offtopic_on:
  248:             # Fix 1: default-ON path deletes ONLY on the topic judge's OFF_SUBJECT stamp
  249:             # (weight labels can never delete; positive relevance vetoes). The legacy
  250:             # weight-label predicate stays reachable ONLY behind the OFF kill-switch so
  251:             # ``PG_DELETE_OFFTOPIC_TOPIC_JUDGE_ONLY=0`` is byte-identical to pre-Fix-1.
  252:             if topic_judge_only_deletion_enabled():
  253:                 if is_row_deletable_offtopic(row, fresh_off_subject_ids=fresh_ids):
  254:                     reason = "confirmed_offtopic_subject"
  255:             elif is_row_confirmed_offtopic(row):
  256:                 reason = "confirmed_offtopic"
  257:         if reason:
  258:             copied = dict(row)
  259:             copied["deletion_reason"] = reason
  260:             deleted.append(copied)
  261:         else:
  262:             kept.append(row)
  263:     return kept, deleted
  264: 
  265: 
  266: def _deletion_signal(reason: str) -> str:
  267:     """Human-readable 'which signal fired' derived from the deletion_reason — a chrome class
  268:     or the topic-judge OFF_SUBJECT stamp. Keeps the disclosure honest about the exact
  269:     category (chrome non-source vs confirmed-off-topic) that removed each row."""
  270:     if reason.startswith("content_integrity_junk"):
  271:         cls = reason.split(":", 1)[1] if ":" in reason else "chrome"
  272:         return "chrome:" + (cls or "chrome")
  273:     if reason.startswith("confirmed_offtopic"):
  274:         return "topic_judge_off_subject"
  275:     return reason or "unknown"
  276: 
  277: 
  278: def _judge_verdict_summary(row: Mapping[str, Any]) -> str:
  279:     """Compact per-source verdict trail the row carried at deletion time (read-only — never a
  280:     delete trigger here). Surfaces WHY the source was judged, so a reviewer can second-guess
  281:     any deletion from the manifest alone."""
  282:     parts: list[str] = []
  283:     if _stamped_off_subject(row):
  284:         parts.append("topic=OFF_SUBJECT")
  285:     if row.get("topic_offtopic_demoted") is True:
  286:         parts.append("topic_offtopic_demoted=True")
  287:     label = str(row.get("content_relevance_label", "") or "").strip()
  288:     if label:
  289:         parts.append("content_relevance_label=" + label)
  290:     verdict = str(row.get("topic_relevance_verdict", "") or "").strip()
  291:     if verdict:
  292:         parts.append("topic_relevance_verdict=" + verdict)
  293:     ci_class = str(row.get("content_integrity_class", "") or "").strip()
  294:     if ci_class:
  295:         parts.append("content_integrity_class=" + ci_class)
  296:     return ";".join(parts)
  297: 
  298: 
  299: def disclosure_records(deleted_rows: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
  300:     """Compact disclosure rows for the run telemetry — the audit trail that proves the
  301:     pipeline found and DELETED each junk / off-topic source (recorded, never silent).
  302: 
  303:     Fix 5 (records half): each record now carries the per-source SIGNAL that fired
  304:     (chrome class vs topic-judge OFF_SUBJECT), the JUDGE VERDICT trail, and the source TIER
  305:     alongside the existing evidence_id / title / url / deletion_reason — enough to second-
  306:     guess any single deletion straight from the manifest (fail-loud, never silent)."""
  307:     out: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
  308:     for row in deleted_rows:
  309:         if not isinstance(row, Mapping):
  310:             continue
  311:         reason = str(row.get("deletion_reason", "") or "")
  312:         out.append({
  313:             "evidence_id": row.get("evidence_id", ""),
  314:             "title": row.get("source_title") or row.get("title") or "",
  315:             "url": row.get("url") or row.get("source_url") or "",
  316:             "tier": row.get("tier") or row.get("source_tier") or "",
  317:             "deletion_reason": reason,
  318:             "signal": _deletion_signal(reason),
  319:             "judge_verdict": _judge_verdict_summary(row),
  320:             "excluded_from_grounding": True,
  321:         })
  322:     return out

  261: def _build_batch_prompt(
  262:     research_question: str,
  263:     batch: list[tuple[int, str, str]],
  264:     *,
  265:     subject_aspect_split: bool = False,
  266: ) -> str:
  267:     """Build a single ON/OFF-topic classification prompt for a batch of
  268:     sources. ``batch`` is a list of (local_index, title, snippet). The LLM is
  269:     asked to return exactly one line per source: ``<index>: ON`` or
  270:     ``<index>: OFF``. Confident-OFF-only is enforced at parse time.
  271: 
  272:     ``subject_aspect_split`` (I-deepfix-003 #1374 Fix 3): when True the OFF verdict
  273:     is split into ``OFF_ASPECT`` (same subject, wrong aspect — kept/demoted) and
  274:     ``OFF_SUBJECT`` (clearly different subject — the only deletable OFF). When False
  275:     (the byte-identical legacy) the prompt asks only for ``ON`` / ``OFF``."""
  276:     # I-deepfix-003 #1374 Fix 3: the STEP-2 rubric, the domain-neutral example, the
  277:     # OUTPUT CONTRACT, and the trailer are the ONLY segments that differ between the
  278:     # legacy two-verdict form and the three-verdict subject/aspect split. Everything
  279:     # else (STEP 1, the date-blind rule, the fail-open) is byte-identical in both. The
  280:     # ``else`` strings below reproduce the legacy prompt EXACTLY (byte-identical OFF).
  281:     if subject_aspect_split:
  282:         step2_line = (
  283:             "STEP 2 — for EACH numbered source below, choose EXACTLY ONE verdict: "
  284:             "ON if the source plausibly bears on BOTH the subject entity AND that "
  285:             "specific aspect; OFF_ASPECT if the source is about the SAME subject "
  286:             "entity but a DIFFERENT aspect / use-case / population than the question "
  287:             "asks about (same subject, wrong question — a topic-adjacent hub that is "
  288:             "KEPT and only demoted, never removed); OFF_SUBJECT if the source is "
  289:             "about a CLEARLY DIFFERENT subject entity (different field, disease, "
  290:             "domain — e.g. an unrelated-domain or scholar-mill paper). When you are "
  291:             "unsure between OFF_ASPECT and OFF_SUBJECT, choose OFF_ASPECT (the "
  292:             "safer, keep-and-demote verdict)."
  293:         )
  294:         example_line = (
  295:             "Example (domain-neutral): if the question is about entity X and aspect "
  296:             "A, then a source about entity X but aspect B is OFF_ASPECT; a source "
  297:             "about a clearly different entity Y is OFF_SUBJECT; a source about entity "
  298:             "X and aspect A is ON."
  299:         )
  300:         output_contract_line = (
  301:             "OUTPUT CONTRACT (strict — the parser accepts nothing else): OUTPUT ONLY "
  302:             "THE VERDICT LINES, exactly one per source, each line EXACTLY in the form "
  303:             "`<index>: ON`, `<index>: OFF_ASPECT`, or `<index>: OFF_SUBJECT`. Do NOT "
  304:             "write the entity or aspect names, any reasoning, any explanation, or any "
  305:             "other words — not on a verdict line and not anywhere else in the output."
  306:         )
  307:         trailer_line = (
  308:             "VERDICTS (one `<index>: ON|OFF_ASPECT|OFF_SUBJECT` line per source):"
  309:         )
  310:     else:
  311:         step2_line = (
  312:             "STEP 2 — for EACH numbered source below, mark it ON only if it plausibly "
  313:             "bears on BOTH the subject entity AND that specific aspect. A source about "
  314:             "the SAME entity but a DIFFERENT aspect / use-case / population than the "
  315:             "question asks about is OFF-TOPIC — same subject, wrong question. A source "
  316:             "about a clearly different subject entity (different field, disease, "
  317:             "population) is also OFF-TOPIC."
  318:         )
  319:         example_line = (
  320:             "Example (domain-neutral): if the question is about entity X and aspect A, "
  321:             "then a source about entity X but aspect B is OFF; a source about entity X "
  322:             "and aspect A is ON."
  323:         )
  324:         output_contract_line = (
  325:             "OUTPUT CONTRACT (strict — the parser accepts nothing else): OUTPUT ONLY "
  326:             "THE VERDICT LINES, exactly one per source, each line EXACTLY in the form "
  327:             "`<index>: ON` or `<index>: OFF`. Do NOT write the entity or aspect names, "
  328:             "any reasoning, any explanation, or any other words — not on a verdict "
  329:             "line and not anywhere else in the output."
  330:         )
  331:         trailer_line = "VERDICTS (one `<index>: ON|OFF` line per source):"
  332:     lines = [
  333:         "You are a strict topic-relevance classifier for a research report.",
  334:         "",
  335:         f"RESEARCH QUESTION:\n{research_question.strip()}",
  336:         "",
  337:         # I-deepfix-001 FF4-ASPECT (v2, forensic-corrected): FACET-SCOPED rubric
  338:         # (was entity-only) + a STRICT verdict-only output contract. An
  339:         # entity-only "different subject?" prompt is structurally blind to a
  340:         # same-entity / wrong-ASPECT source (e.g. a GenAI-in-education paper
  341:         # grounding a GenAI-labor-market question): the shared entity satisfies
  342:         # "not a different field" and the fail-open keeps it ON. The two-step
  343:         # rubric below makes the model name the question's SUBJECT ENTITY *and*
  344:         # its SPECIFIC ASPECT *silently* (internal reasoning only), then requires
  345:         # a source to bear on BOTH. It is domain-agnostic (LAW VI — the aspect is
  346:         # derived at runtime from the RESEARCH QUESTION; nothing domain-specific
  347:         # is hardcoded) and preserves the explicit fail-open.
  348:         #
  349:         # FORENSIC ADJUSTMENT #2 (off-topic fix_change_needed): the entity+aspect
  350:         # naming MUST stay INTERNAL and the output MUST be strictly one
  351:         # `<index>: ON|OFF` line per source and nothing else. Inline reasoning on
  352:         # a verdict line ("1: this is about L2 writing, OFF") is not recognised by
  353:         # _parse_batch_verdicts (below, unchanged) -> count mismatch -> the WHOLE
  354:         # batch fails OPEN, silently letting the off-aspect source survive. So the
  355:         # output contract is hardened here rather than the parser being relaxed.
  356:         "STEP 1 (do this SILENTLY — this reasoning must NOT appear anywhere in "
  357:         "your output): read the RESEARCH QUESTION and name to yourself its two "
  358:         "parts — the SUBJECT ENTITY it is about, and the SPECIFIC ASPECT it asks "
  359:         "about that entity (the outcome, relation, sub-domain, use-case, or "
  360:         "population the question is actually asking about).",
  361:         "",
  362:         step2_line,
  363:         "",
  364:         example_line,
  365:         "",
  366:         # I-deepfix-001 (drb_72 forensic): the seminal on-topic papers were wrongly marked OFF
  367:         # because the question text embeds a DATE window ("before June 2023") and the judge read a
  368:         # post-cutoff date/marker in a snippet as a "different aspect". TOPICALITY IS DATE-BLIND.
  369:         "TOPICALITY IS DATE-BLIND: a publication date — or ANY date in the research question — is "
  370:         "NOT an aspect. NEVER mark a source OFF because of its publication date or a date range in "
  371:         "the question; recency is a SEPARATE axis handled elsewhere. Judge ONLY subject-entity + "
  372:         "aspect. An exposure / projection / potential-impact / early-evidence study of the "
  373:         "question's aspect is ON (it bears on that aspect), not OFF.",
  374:         "",
  375:         "FAIL-OPEN: if you genuinely cannot tell whether the source addresses the "
  376:         "question's specific aspect, mark it ON. When in doubt, answer ON.",
  377:         "",
  378:         output_contract_line,
  379:         "",
  380:         "SOURCES:",
  381:     ]
  382:     for local_idx, title, snippet in batch:
  383:         text = title.strip()
  384:         if snippet:
  385:             text = f"{text} — {snippet}" if text else snippet
  386:         if not text:
  387:             text = "(no title or snippet)"
  388:         lines.append(f"{local_idx}: {text}")
  389:     lines.append("")
  390:     lines.append(trailer_line)
  391:     return "\n".join(lines)
  392: 
  393: 
  394: def _parse_batch_verdicts(
  395:     raw: str,
  396:     expected_indices: list[int],
  397: ) -> dict[int, bool] | None:
  398:     """Parse the LLM batch response into ``{local_index: is_offtopic}``.
  399: 
  400:     Returns None (FAIL-OPEN signal — keep the whole batch) when the parse is
  401:     not exactly one recognised verdict per requested index. A recognised
  402:     verdict line is ``<index>: ON`` or ``<index>: OFF`` (case-insensitive,
  403:     tolerant of surrounding punctuation). Anything else => fail-open."""
  404:     if not isinstance(raw, str) or not raw.strip():
  405:         return None
  406:     verdicts: dict[int, bool] = {}
  407:     wanted = set(expected_indices)
  408:     for line in raw.splitlines():
  409:         stripped = line.strip()
  410:         if not stripped or ":" not in stripped:
  411:             continue
  412:         idx_part, _, verdict_part = stripped.partition(":")
  413:         idx_token = idx_part.strip().lstrip("-").strip()
  414:         if not idx_token.isdigit():
  415:             continue
  416:         idx = int(idx_token)
  417:         if idx not in wanted:
  418:             continue
  419:         verdict_token = verdict_part.strip().lower()
  420:         # Confident ON / confident OFF only. Anything ambiguous is ignored
  421:         # (so the count check below will trip fail-open).
  422:         if verdict_token.startswith("on"):
  423:             verdicts[idx] = False
  424:         elif verdict_token.startswith("off"):
  425:             verdicts[idx] = True
  426:         # else: leave unset -> count mismatch -> fail-open
  427:     if set(verdicts.keys()) != wanted:
  428:         # Missing / extra / unparseable verdicts: keep the whole batch.
  429:         return None
  430:     return verdicts
  431: 
  432: 
  433: def _parse_batch_verdicts_split(
  434:     raw: str,
  435:     expected_indices: list[int],
  436: ) -> dict[int, str] | None:
  437:     """Parse the three-verdict (subject/aspect split) LLM response into
  438:     ``{local_index: "ON" | "OFF_ASPECT" | "OFF_SUBJECT"}``.
  439: 
  440:     Returns None (FAIL-OPEN — keep the whole batch) on the SAME conditions as the
  441:     legacy :func:`_parse_batch_verdicts`: empty/blank input, or any result that is
  442:     not exactly one recognised verdict per requested index. Recognised verdict
  443:     tokens (case-insensitive, separator-tolerant so ``off subject`` / ``off-subject``
  444:     / ``off_subject`` all match): ``on`` -> ON, ``off_subject`` -> OFF_SUBJECT,
  445:     ``off_aspect`` -> OFF_ASPECT, and a legacy bare ``off`` -> OFF_ASPECT
  446:     (conservative — the old verdict form is NEVER treated as deletable). Anything
  447:     unrecognised is ignored so the count check below trips fail-open."""
  448:     if not isinstance(raw, str) or not raw.strip():
  449:         return None
  450:     verdicts: dict[int, str] = {}
  725:         )
  726: 
  727:     return TopicGateResult(
  728:         kept_rows=kept_rows,
  729:         dropped_rows=dropped_rows,
  730:         dropped_titles=dropped_titles,
  731:         n_in=n_in,
  732:         n_kept=len(kept_rows),
  733:         n_dropped_offtopic=len(dropped_rows),
  734:         n_exempt=len(exempt_rows),
  735:         notes=notes,
  736:         demoted_rows=demoted_rows,
  737:         demoted_titles=demoted_titles,
  738:         n_demoted_offtopic=len(demoted_rows),
  739:     )

+def _attach_junk_deletion_disclosure(manifest: dict, run_dir: "Path | None") -> dict:
+    """I-deepfix-003 (#1374) Fix 5: attach the split junk-deletion disclosure
+    (``deleted_chrome_nonsources`` + ``deleted_offtopic_sources``) to ``manifest`` from the
+    DURABLE ``run_dir/junk_deletion_disclosure.json`` the seam wrote. Called from
+    ``_attach_tool_utilization`` so EVERY manifest write path (success + every abort/error site)
+    carries it — a deletion is never silent (§-1.3.1 fail-loud), and the deleted_* keys land on
+    abort manifests too.
+
+    Keys are attached ONLY when the durable file EXISTS (i.e. the seam actually ran this pass):
+    a pre-seam abort leaves the manifest byte-identical (no keys), so this never changes an
+    abort shape for a run that never reached the gate. ``deleted_offtopic_sources`` matches ANY
+    ``confirmed_offtopic*`` reason (Fix 1 emits ``confirmed_offtopic_subject``; the legacy path
+    emits ``confirmed_offtopic``) — the prior ``== "confirmed_offtopic"`` filter silently MISSED
+    the Fix-1 reason. FAIL-OPEN: any error leaves the manifest untouched (never abort a run for
+    a disclosure read)."""
+    try:
+        if run_dir is None:
+            return manifest
+        _p = Path(run_dir) / "junk_deletion_disclosure.json"
+        if not _p.is_file():
+            return manifest  # gate did not run this pass — byte-identical (no keys)
+        _payload = json.loads(_p.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
+        _recs = _payload.get("deleted", []) if isinstance(_payload, dict) else []
+        if not isinstance(_recs, list):
+            _recs = []
+        manifest["deleted_chrome_nonsources"] = [
+            r for r in _recs
+            if isinstance(r, dict)
+            and str(r.get("deletion_reason", "")).startswith("content_integrity_junk")
+        ]
+        manifest["deleted_offtopic_sources"] = [
+            r for r in _recs
+            if isinstance(r, dict)
+            and str(r.get("deletion_reason", "")).startswith("confirmed_offtopic")
+        ]
+    except Exception as _jd_disc_exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — disclosure attach must never abort a run
+        print(f"[junk-deletion-gate] disclosure attach skipped: {_jd_disc_exc}")
+    return manifest
+

+def topic_gate_subject_aspect_split_enabled() -> bool:
+    """Flag ``PG_TOPIC_GATE_SUBJECT_ASPECT_SPLIT`` (default ON — I-deepfix-003 #1374 Fix 3).
+
+    Splits the single confident-OFF verdict into two kinds:
+      - ``OFF_ASPECT`` — the SAME subject entity but a DIFFERENT aspect / use-case /
+        population than the question asks about (a topic-adjacent hub, e.g. an
+        education-AI paper for a labor-market question). DEMOTE-and-keep, NEVER deletable.
+      - ``OFF_SUBJECT`` — a CLEARLY DIFFERENT subject entity (different field / domain —
+        scholar-mill / unrelated-domain junk). This is the ONLY deletable OFF: it alone
+        carries the ``topic_off_subject=True`` sidecar the downstream junk-deletion gate
+        keys on.
+    A legacy plain ``OFF`` parses as OFF_ASPECT (conservative — never delete on the old
+    verdict form). Set ``PG_TOPIC_GATE_SUBJECT_ASPECT_SPLIT=0`` to restore the
+    byte-identical legacy ON/OFF prompt + parser (no ``topic_off_subject`` stamp)."""
+    raw = os.environ.get("PG_TOPIC_GATE_SUBJECT_ASPECT_SPLIT", "1").strip().lower()
+    return raw not in ("0", "false", "no", "off", "")
+
+
+def junk_chrome_before_offtopic_enabled() -> bool:
+    """Flag ``PG_JUNK_CHROME_BEFORE_OFFTOPIC`` (default ON — I-deepfix-003 #1374 Fix 4).
+
+    A chrome non-source (bot/captcha/cookie/404/login/empty — a FAILED FETCH, not a source)
+    has nothing real to judge for topicality. When ON, such a row is NOT sent to the topic
+    judge at all: it is KEPT (flows to the downstream content-integrity stamp + chrome-delete
+    leg) and is NEVER stamped ``topic_off_subject`` / ``topic_offtopic_demoted``, so a garbled
+    body + a chrome title can never be mislabeled ``confirmed_offtopic`` (Cause 3). OFF =>
+    byte-identical legacy (every non-exempt row with judgeable text is judged)."""
+    raw = os.environ.get("PG_JUNK_CHROME_BEFORE_OFFTOPIC", "1").strip().lower()
+    return raw not in ("0", "false", "no", "off", "")
+
+
+# Content fields scanned (widest-first) for the chrome detector — mirrors the
+# run_honest_sweep_r3 content-integrity stamp pass so the two screens judge the SAME body.
+_CHROME_BODY_FIELDS = (
+    "fetched_body", "full_text", "content", "extracted_text", "raw_content",
+    "raw_text", "page_text", "direct_quote", "statement", "source_text", "body", "text",
+)
+
+
+def _row_is_chrome_nonsource(row: dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
+    """True iff the CONTENT-INTEGRITY detector confirms this row is a chrome non-source
+    (bot/captcha/cookie/404/login/empty). Reads a pre-existing ``content_integrity_junk``
+    stamp first (cheap), else runs the pure leaf detector on the WIDEST body + url + title
+    (the long-body Zyte-recovery guard inside the detector protects a real source whose title
+    is a stale bot page). FAIL-OPEN: any import / error / non-dict => False (row is judged
+    normally — a detector bug must never silently skip a real source)."""
+    try:
+        if not isinstance(row, dict):
+            return False
+        v = row.get("content_integrity_junk")
+        if bool(v) and str(v).strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "no", "off", ""):
+            return True
+        from src.tools.access_bypass import (  # noqa: PLC0415
+            detect_content_integrity_junk as _detect_ci_junk,
+        )
+        body = max(
+            (str(row.get(_bk) or "") for _bk in _CHROME_BODY_FIELDS),
+            key=len, default="",
+        )
+        url = str(row.get("source_url") or row.get("url") or "")
+        title = str(row.get("title") or row.get("source_title") or row.get("statement") or "")
+        is_junk, _cls = _detect_ci_junk(body, url, title)
+        return bool(is_junk)
+    except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — a detector defect must never skip a real source
+        return False
+

 def _build_batch_prompt(
     research_question: str,
     batch: list[tuple[int, str, str]],
+    *,
+    subject_aspect_split: bool = False,
 ) -> str:
     """Build a single ON/OFF-topic classification prompt for a batch of
     sources. ``batch`` is a list of (local_index, title, snippet). The LLM is
     asked to return exactly one line per source: ``<index>: ON`` or
-    ``<index>: OFF``. Confident-OFF-only is enforced at parse time."""
+    ``<index>: OFF``. Confident-OFF-only is enforced at parse time.
+
+    ``subject_aspect_split`` (I-deepfix-003 #1374 Fix 3): when True the OFF verdict
+    is split into ``OFF_ASPECT`` (same subject, wrong aspect — kept/demoted) and
+    ``OFF_SUBJECT`` (clearly different subject — the only deletable OFF). When False
+    (the byte-identical legacy) the prompt asks only for ``ON`` / ``OFF``."""
+    # I-deepfix-003 #1374 Fix 3: the STEP-2 rubric, the domain-neutral example, the
+    # OUTPUT CONTRACT, and the trailer are the ONLY segments that differ between the
+    # legacy two-verdict form and the three-verdict subject/aspect split. Everything
+    # else (STEP 1, the date-blind rule, the fail-open) is byte-identical in both. The
+    # ``else`` strings below reproduce the legacy prompt EXACTLY (byte-identical OFF).
+    if subject_aspect_split:
+        step2_line = (
+            "STEP 2 — for EACH numbered source below, choose EXACTLY ONE verdict: "
+            "ON if the source plausibly bears on BOTH the subject entity AND that "
+            "specific aspect; OFF_ASPECT if the source is about the SAME subject "
+            "entity but a DIFFERENT aspect / use-case / population than the question "
+            "asks about (same subject, wrong question — a topic-adjacent hub that is "
+            "KEPT and only demoted, never removed); OFF_SUBJECT if the source is "
+            "about a CLEARLY DIFFERENT subject entity (different field, disease, "
+            "domain — e.g. an unrelated-domain or scholar-mill paper). When you are "
+            "unsure between OFF_ASPECT and OFF_SUBJECT, choose OFF_ASPECT (the "
+            "safer, keep-and-demote verdict)."
+        )
+        example_line = (
+            "Example (domain-neutral): if the question is about entity X and aspect "
+            "A, then a source about entity X but aspect B is OFF_ASPECT; a source "
+            "about a clearly different entity Y is OFF_SUBJECT; a source about entity "
+            "X and aspect A is ON."
+        )
+        output_contract_line = (
+            "OUTPUT CONTRACT (strict — the parser accepts nothing else): OUTPUT ONLY "
+            "THE VERDICT LINES, exactly one per source, each line EXACTLY in the form "
+            "`<index>: ON`, `<index>: OFF_ASPECT`, or `<index>: OFF_SUBJECT`. Do NOT "
+            "write the entity or aspect names, any reasoning, any explanation, or any "
+            "other words — not on a verdict line and not anywhere else in the output."
+        )
+        trailer_line = (
+            "VERDICTS (one `<index>: ON|OFF_ASPECT|OFF_SUBJECT` line per source):"
+        )
+    else:
+        step2_line = (
+            "STEP 2 — for EACH numbered source below, mark it ON only if it plausibly "
+            "bears on BOTH the subject entity AND that specific aspect. A source about "
+            "the SAME entity but a DIFFERENT aspect / use-case / population than the "
+            "question asks about is OFF-TOPIC — same subject, wrong question. A source "
+            "about a clearly different subject entity (different field, disease, "
+            "population) is also OFF-TOPIC."
+        )
+        example_line = (
+            "Example (domain-neutral): if the question is about entity X and aspect A, "
+            "then a source about entity X but aspect B is OFF; a source about entity X "
+            "and aspect A is ON."
+        )

+def _parse_batch_verdicts_split(
+    raw: str,
+    expected_indices: list[int],
+) -> dict[int, str] | None:
+    """Parse the three-verdict (subject/aspect split) LLM response into
+    ``{local_index: "ON" | "OFF_ASPECT" | "OFF_SUBJECT"}``.
+
+    Returns None (FAIL-OPEN — keep the whole batch) on the SAME conditions as the
+    legacy :func:`_parse_batch_verdicts`: empty/blank input, or any result that is
+    not exactly one recognised verdict per requested index. Recognised verdict
+    tokens (case-insensitive, separator-tolerant so ``off subject`` / ``off-subject``
+    / ``off_subject`` all match): ``on`` -> ON, ``off_subject`` -> OFF_SUBJECT,
+    ``off_aspect`` -> OFF_ASPECT, and a legacy bare ``off`` -> OFF_ASPECT
+    (conservative — the old verdict form is NEVER treated as deletable). Anything
+    unrecognised is ignored so the count check below trips fail-open."""
+    if not isinstance(raw, str) or not raw.strip():
+        return None
+    verdicts: dict[int, str] = {}
+    wanted = set(expected_indices)
+    for line in raw.splitlines():
+        stripped = line.strip()
+        if not stripped or ":" not in stripped:
+            continue
+        idx_part, _, verdict_part = stripped.partition(":")
+        idx_token = idx_part.strip().lstrip("-").strip()
+        if not idx_token.isdigit():
+            continue
+        idx = int(idx_token)
+        if idx not in wanted:
+            continue
+        # Normalise separators so "off subject"/"off-subject"/"off_subject" collapse.
+        norm = verdict_part.strip().lower().replace("-", "_").replace(" ", "_")
+        if norm.startswith("on"):
+            verdicts[idx] = "ON"
+        elif norm.startswith("off_subject") or norm.startswith("offsubject"):
+            verdicts[idx] = "OFF_SUBJECT"
+        elif norm.startswith("off_aspect") or norm.startswith("offaspect"):
+            verdicts[idx] = "OFF_ASPECT"
+        elif norm.startswith("off"):
+            # Legacy bare OFF -> OFF_ASPECT (conservative: never delete on the
+            # old verdict form).
+            verdicts[idx] = "OFF_ASPECT"
+        # else: unrecognised -> leave unset -> count mismatch -> fail-open.
+    if set(verdicts.keys()) != wanted:
+        return None
+    return verdicts
+
+

     sources: list[dict[str, Any]],
     research_question: str,

+# ── Fix 1: topic-judge-only off-topic DELETE predicate (default ON) ──────────────────────
+# A weight/reranker ``content_relevance_label`` can NEVER delete; a positive relevance
+# verdict vetoes unconditionally; only the topic judge's OFF_SUBJECT stamp deletes; missing
+# verdict fails open (KEEP). These are the 4 confirmed I-deepfix-003 victim shapes.
+
+def _label_demoted():
+    # topic judge said ON (no OFF stamp) but the reranker demoted the numeric score. This is
+    # the 197-row leak shape: Fed / OECD / ILO / McKinsey / Wikipedia all died on this label.
+    return {"evidence_id": "ev_demoted", "title": "OECD Employment Outlook",
+            "content_relevance_label": "demoted"}

+def _fresh_off_subject():
+    return {"evidence_id": "ev_subj", "title": "Reconceptualising tourism co-creation",
+            "topic_off_subject": True, "topic_relevance_verdict": "OFF_SUBJECT", "tier": "T6"}
+
+
+def _positive_plus_stale_off():
+    # judges disagree: content-relevance judge affirmatively said RELEVANT, a stale topic
+    # stamp says OFF. The positive verdict must win (KEEP).
+    return {"evidence_id": "ev_pos", "title": "Generative AI at Work",
+            "content_relevance_label": "relevant", "topic_off_subject": True,
+            "topic_offtopic_demoted": True}
+

+    assert jd.is_row_deletable_offtopic({"topic_off_subject": "off_subject"}) is True
+    assert jd.is_row_deletable_offtopic({"topic_offtopic_demoted": True}) is False

+def test_deletable_predicate_positive_verdict_vetoes():
+    assert jd.is_row_deletable_offtopic(_positive_plus_stale_off()) is False

+    assert jd.is_row_deletable_offtopic(_clean()) is False
+    assert jd.is_row_deletable_offtopic("not-a-mapping") is False

+def test_partition_topic_judge_only_default_on(monkeypatch):

+    kept, deleted = jd.partition_rows(rows)

+def test_partition_off_subject_never_deletes_weight_label(monkeypatch):

  481: def classify_topic_relevance(
  482:     sources: list[dict[str, Any]],
  483:     research_question: str,
  484:     llm_callable: Callable[[str], str],
  485:     *,
  486:     batch_size: int | None = None,
  487:     primary_trial_anchors: list[str] | None = None,
  488:     anchor_predicate: Callable[[dict[str, Any]], bool] | None = None,
  489: ) -> TopicGateResult:
  490:     """Drop sources CONFIDENTLY classified OFF-topic for the research question.
  491: 
  492:     Pure + side-effect-free (apart from logging): the caller supplies the LLM
  493:     via ``llm_callable(prompt: str) -> str`` so this is fully unit-testable
  494:     with a stub. Marquee / required-entity anchors are EXEMPT (never dropped).
  495:     FAIL-OPEN: any LLM exception, count mismatch, or unparseable verdict keeps
  496:     the whole batch. Drops ONLY on an explicit confident OFF verdict.
  497: 
  498:     Args:
  499:         sources: evidence rows (selection-stage, post floor + dedup).
  500:         research_question: the user's raw question (the topic anchor).
  501:         llm_callable: synchronous ``str -> str`` LLM interface.
  502:         batch_size: sources per LLM call (default :func:`topic_batch_size`).
  503:         primary_trial_anchors: named-trial anchors; a row matching one is
  504:             exempt (handled via ``anchor_predicate`` when supplied).
  505:         anchor_predicate: optional extra "is this a primary anchor" test
  506:             (the orchestrator passes the selector's anchor matcher so the
  507:             exemption is identical to the floor stage). Marquee detection is
  508:             always applied in addition.
  509: 
  510:     Returns:
  511:         TopicGateResult with kept/dropped rows + honest telemetry.
  512:     """
  513:     n_in = len(sources)
  514:     if n_in == 0:
  515:         return TopicGateResult(
  516:             kept_rows=[], dropped_rows=[], n_in=0, n_kept=0,
  517:             n_dropped_offtopic=0, notes=["topic_gate: empty pool"],
  518:         )
  519:     if not (research_question or "").strip():
  520:         # Nothing to anchor on — FAIL-OPEN, keep everything.
  521:         return TopicGateResult(
  522:             kept_rows=list(sources), dropped_rows=[], n_in=n_in,
  523:             n_kept=n_in, n_dropped_offtopic=0,
  524:             notes=["topic_gate: empty research_question — fail-open"],
  525:         )

  527:     size = batch_size if (batch_size and batch_size > 0) else topic_batch_size()

+# delete. DEFAULT ON. OFF => byte-identical legacy weight-label path.
+_TOPIC_JUDGE_ONLY_FLAG = "PG_DELETE_OFFTOPIC_TOPIC_JUDGE_ONLY"
+# Fix 2 (I-deepfix-003 over-deletion): the off-topic DELETE fires ONLY on an OFF_SUBJECT
+# stamp THIS run's topic judge produced. A STALE stamp reloaded from an earlier run's
+# corpus_snapshot (the judge did NOT re-run this pass) demote-KEEPs. DEFAULT ON. OFF =>
+# freshness is NOT enforced (byte-identical to the Fix-1-only path: any OFF_SUBJECT stamp
+# deletes regardless of provenance).
+_FRESH_VERDICT_FLAG = "PG_DELETE_OFFTOPIC_FRESH_VERDICT_ONLY"
 _OFF_VALUES = frozenset({"0", "false", "no", "off", "disabled", ""})
 
+# An affirmative positive-relevance verdict from the content-relevance judge. A row carrying
+# one is on-topic by the judge's own word and VETOES deletion unconditionally.
+_POSITIVE_RELEVANCE_LABELS = frozenset({"relevant", "escalated_relevant"})
+# String forms that mean an affirmative OFF_SUBJECT stamp (the deletable class of the OFF
+# split). ``topic_off_subject`` is normally the bool True (Fix 3 sidecar); these tolerate a
+# string representation without ever matching OFF_ASPECT or a weight label.
+_OFF_SUBJECT_TRUE_TOKENS = frozenset({"off_subject", "offsubject", "true", "yes", "on", "1"})

+def topic_judge_only_deletion_enabled() -> bool:

+    DELETE fires ONLY on the topic judge's affirmative OFF_SUBJECT stamp

+def fresh_verdict_only_deletion_enabled() -> bool:

+def _stamped_off_subject(row: Mapping[str, Any]) -> bool:
+    """True iff the topic judge stamped this WHOLE source OFF_SUBJECT — a clearly different
+    subject (the DELETABLE class of the OFF split, e.g. a scholar-mill / tourism / religion
+    page in an AI-labor report). The Fix-3 sidecar is the bool ``topic_off_subject=True``; a
+    string verdict ``topic_relevance_verdict == "OFF_SUBJECT"`` is tolerated as the same
+    signal. Legacy ``topic_offtopic_demoted`` alone (which conflates OFF_ASPECT 'same entity,
+    wrong aspect' with OFF_SUBJECT) does NOT count — a demote-keep aspect verdict is never a
+    delete trigger, so only the explicit subject-level stamp deletes."""
+    v = row.get("topic_off_subject")
+    if v is True:
+        return True
+    if isinstance(v, str) and v.strip().lower() in _OFF_SUBJECT_TRUE_TOKENS:
+        return True
+    verdict = str(row.get("topic_relevance_verdict", "") or "").strip().lower()
+    return verdict == "off_subject"
+
+
+def is_row_deletable_offtopic(
+    row: Mapping[str, Any],
+    fresh_off_subject_ids: "Iterable[str] | None" = None,
+) -> bool:
+    """DELETE predicate for the confirmed-off-topic class (topic-judge-only path, Fix 1 + Fix 2).
+
+    Returns True (row is DELETABLE) iff the topic judge AFFIRMATIVELY stamped this WHOLE
+    source OFF_SUBJECT. Three hard guarantees keep this from over-deleting:
+
+    * A weight/reranker ``content_relevance_label`` (``demoted`` / ``escalated_demoted``) is
+      NEVER a delete trigger — those are weight-demote-to-0.25 KEEP labels (a Qwen3-Reranker
+      numeric score / a GLM 'INSUFFICIENT' entailment), NOT topic verdicts. Reusing them as a
+      DELETE trigger is exactly what hard-deleted 197 on-topic rows (St. Louis Fed, OECD, ILO,
+      McKinsey, HBS, Wikipedia, 23 T1 journal papers) in the I-deepfix-003 pass.
+    * An affirmative positive-relevance verdict (``content_relevance_label`` in
+      {relevant, escalated_relevant}) VETOES deletion UNCONDITIONALLY — even against a
+      stale/false OFF stamp. When the two judges disagree, the positive relevance wins.
+    * Fix 2 (fresh-verdict-only): when ``fresh_off_subject_ids`` is supplied (a concrete set —
+      the evidence_ids THIS run's topic judge freshly confirmed OFF_SUBJECT) AND
+      ``PG_DELETE_OFFTOPIC_FRESH_VERDICT_ONLY`` is ON, a row whose OFF_SUBJECT stamp is NOT in
+      that set is a STALE snapshot stamp (an earlier run's verdict reloaded from
+      corpus_snapshot) and demote-KEEPs — only a fresh verdict deletes. ``None`` (the default)
+      => freshness is un-enforced (byte-identical to the Fix-1-only path).
+
+    FAIL-OPEN: not a Mapping / no OFF_SUBJECT stamp / stale-only stamp / missing verdict / any
+    error => NOT deletable (row KEPT). A predicate bug must NEVER delete a source."""
+    try:
+        if not isinstance(row, Mapping):
+            return False
+        label = str(row.get("content_relevance_label", "") or "").strip().lower()
+        if label in _POSITIVE_RELEVANCE_LABELS:
+            return False  # affirmative positive-relevance verdict — KEEP (unconditional veto)
+        if not _stamped_off_subject(row):
+            return False
+        # Fix 2: a STALE snapshot OFF_SUBJECT stamp (not in this run's fresh set) demote-KEEPs.
+        # Enforced only when the caller passes a concrete set AND the flag is ON.
+        if fresh_off_subject_ids is not None and fresh_verdict_only_deletion_enabled():
+            eid = str(row.get("evidence_id", "") or "")
+            if eid not in {str(e) for e in fresh_off_subject_ids}:
+                return False  # stale stamp — demote-keep, never delete on an old verdict
+        return True
+    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — never delete on a predicate bug
+        logger.warning(
+            "[junk_deletion_gate] deletable-offtopic predicate errored (%s) — row KEPT "
+            "(fail-open).", str(exc)[:160],
+        )
+        return False
+
+

+def _deletion_signal(reason: str) -> str:
+    """Human-readable 'which signal fired' derived from the deletion_reason — a chrome class
+    or the topic-judge OFF_SUBJECT stamp. Keeps the disclosure honest about the exact
+    category (chrome non-source vs confirmed-off-topic) that removed each row."""
+    if reason.startswith("content_integrity_junk"):
+        cls = reason.split(":", 1)[1] if ":" in reason else "chrome"
+        return "chrome:" + (cls or "chrome")
+    if reason.startswith("confirmed_offtopic"):
+        return "topic_judge_off_subject"
+    return reason or "unknown"
+
+
+def _judge_verdict_summary(row: Mapping[str, Any]) -> str:
+    """Compact per-source verdict trail the row carried at deletion time (read-only — never a
+    delete trigger here). Surfaces WHY the source was judged, so a reviewer can second-guess
+    any deletion from the manifest alone."""
+    parts: list[str] = []
+    if _stamped_off_subject(row):
+        parts.append("topic=OFF_SUBJECT")
+    if row.get("topic_offtopic_demoted") is True:
+        parts.append("topic_offtopic_demoted=True")
+    label = str(row.get("content_relevance_label", "") or "").strip()
+    if label:
+        parts.append("content_relevance_label=" + label)
+    verdict = str(row.get("topic_relevance_verdict", "") or "").strip()
+    if verdict:
+        parts.append("topic_relevance_verdict=" + verdict)
+    ci_class = str(row.get("content_integrity_class", "") or "").strip()
+    if ci_class:
+        parts.append("content_integrity_class=" + ci_class)
+    return ";".join(parts)

    2: 
    3: ROOT DEFECT (over-deletion): the topic gate emitted a single ``OFF`` verdict, and the
    4: downstream junk-deletion gate treated every OFF/demoted source as deletable. But most
    5: OFF rows are OFF_ASPECT — the SAME subject entity, a DIFFERENT aspect (an education-AI
    6: paper, an HBR hub for a labor-market question). Deleting those is the over-deletion bug:
    7: 40-48% of deleted rows were topic-adjacent hubs / on-topic sources, not junk.
    8: 
    9: THE FIX (Fix 3): the topic prompt now returns ``ON | OFF_ASPECT | OFF_SUBJECT``.
   10:   * OFF_SUBJECT = a clearly DIFFERENT subject (scholar-mill / unrelated-domain junk) —
   11:     the ONLY deletable OFF. It carries the ``topic_off_subject=True`` sidecar the
   12:     junk-deletion gate keys deletion on.
   13:   * OFF_ASPECT = same entity, wrong aspect (a topic hub) — DEMOTED-and-kept, NEVER
   14:     deletable (``topic_offtopic_demoted=True`` only, no ``topic_off_subject``).
   15:   * A legacy bare ``OFF`` parses as OFF_ASPECT (conservative — never delete on the old

   45: @pytest.fixture(autouse=True)
   46: def _split_env(monkeypatch):
   47:     """Default the split ON for these tests, independent of any leaked env."""
   48:     monkeypatch.setenv("PG_TOPIC_GATE_SUBJECT_ASPECT_SPLIT", "1")
   49:     yield
   50: 
   51: 
   52: def _split_llm(prompt: str) -> str:
   53:     """A competent-model stub that answers the three-verdict split contract.
   54: 
   55:     Reads the SOURCES block the gate built and returns one ``<idx>: <verdict>`` line
   56:     per source (verdict-only). Decision by markers:
   57:       * labor / employment source  -> ON
   58:       * a clearly different subject (blockchain / supply-chain) -> OFF_SUBJECT
   59:       * a same-entity wrong-aspect source (classroom / L2 writing) -> OFF_ASPECT
   60:       * otherwise -> ON (fail-open)
   61:     """
   62:     labor = ("employment", "wage", "job displacement", "labor market", "labour")
   63:     off_subject = ("blockchain", "supply-chain", "supply chain")
   64:     off_aspect = ("classroom", "l2 writing", "perceptions", "students")
   65:     out: list[str] = []
   66:     in_sources = False
   67:     for raw_line in prompt.splitlines():
   68:         line = raw_line.strip()
   69:         if line == "SOURCES:":
   70:             in_sources = True
   71:             continue
   72:         if not in_sources or ":" not in line:
   73:             continue
   74:         idx_part, _, text = line.partition(":")
   75:         idx = idx_part.strip()
   76:         if not idx.isdigit():
   77:             continue  # skips the trailing "VERDICTS (...)" trailer
   78:         low = text.lower()
   79:         if any(k in low for k in labor):
   80:             out.append(f"{idx}: ON")
   81:         elif any(k in low for k in off_subject):
   82:             out.append(f"{idx}: OFF_SUBJECT")
   83:         elif any(k in low for k in off_aspect):
   84:             out.append(f"{idx}: OFF_ASPECT")
   85:         else:
   86:             out.append(f"{idx}: ON")
   87:     return "\n".join(out)

   22: 
   23: def _stub_all_off_subject(prompt: str) -> str:
   24:     """A stub LLM that marks EVERY judged source OFF_SUBJECT (one verdict line per source
   25:     index found in the prompt's SOURCES block), so any row that reaches the judge gets the
   26:     deletable stamp — the test then proves a chrome row NEVER reaches it."""
   27:     idxs: list[int] = []
   28:     in_sources = False
   29:     for line in prompt.splitlines():
   30:         if line.strip() == "SOURCES:":
   31:             in_sources = True
   32:             continue
   33:         if in_sources:
   34:             m = re.match(r"^(\d+):", line.strip())
   35:             if m:
   36:                 idxs.append(int(m.group(1)))
   37:     return "\n".join(f"{i}: OFF_SUBJECT" for i in idxs)

  134: def _offtopic_relevance_override_enabled() -> bool:
  135:     """Kill-switch ``PG_OFFTOPIC_RELEVANCE_OVERRIDE`` (default ON). OFF => the
  136:     legacy byte-identical ``_is_confirmed_offtopic`` (topic-flag wins)."""
  137:     return os.environ.get("PG_OFFTOPIC_RELEVANCE_OVERRIDE", "1").strip().lower() not in (
  138:         "0", "false", "no", "off",
  139:     )
